Use when user wants to turn advice, lessons, or educational content into concrete action steps, reps, or a learning quest.</div></td>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Ship-Learn-Next Action Planner</h1><a id="user-content-ship-learn-next-action-planner" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Ship-Learn-Next Action Planner" href="#ship-learn-next-action-planner"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This skill helps transform passive learning content into actionable <strong>Ship-Learn-Next cycles</strong> - turning advice and lessons into concrete, shippable iterations.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">When to Use This Skill</h2><a id="user-content-when-to-use-this-skill" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: When to Use This Skill" href="#when-to-use-this-skill"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Activate when the user:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Has a transcript/article/tutorial and wants to "implement the advice"</li>
<li>Asks to "turn this into a plan" or "make this actionable"</li>
<li>Wants to extract implementation steps from educational content</li>
<li>Needs help breaking down big ideas into small, shippable reps</li>
<li>Says things like "I watched/read X, now what should I do?"</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Core Framework: Ship-Learn-Next</h2><a id="user-content-core-framework-ship-learn-next" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Core Framework: Ship-Learn-Next" href="#core-framework-ship-learn-next"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Every learning quest follows three repeating phases:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>SHIP</strong> - Create something real (code, content, product, demonstration)</li>
<li><strong>LEARN</strong> - Honest reflection on what happened</li>
<li><strong>NEXT</strong> - Plan the next iteration based on learnings</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Key principle</strong>: 100 reps beats 100 hours of study. Learning = doing better, not knowing more.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How This Skill Works</h2><a id="user-content-how-this-skill-works" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How This Skill Works" href="#how-this-skill-works"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 1: Read the Content</h3><a id="user-content-step-1-read-the-content" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 1: Read the Content" href="#step-1-read-the-content"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Read the file the user provides (transcript, article, notes):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# User provides path to file
FILE_PATH=&quot;/path/to/content.txt&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> User provides path to file</span>
FILE_PATH=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>/path/to/content.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Use the Read tool to analyze the content.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 2: Extract Core Lessons</h3><a id="user-content-step-2-extract-core-lessons" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 2: Extract Core Lessons" href="#step-2-extract-core-lessons"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Identify from the content:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Main advice/lessons</strong>: What are the key takeaways?</li>
<li><strong>Actionable principles</strong>: What can actually be practiced?</li>
<li><strong>Skills being taught</strong>: What would someone learn by doing this?</li>
<li><strong>Examples/case studies</strong>: Real implementations mentioned</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Do NOT</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Summarize everything (focus on actionable parts)</li>
<li>List theory without application</li>
<li>Include "nice to know" vs "need to practice"</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 3: Define the Quest</h3><a id="user-content-step-3-define-the-quest" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 3: Define the Quest" href="#step-3-define-the-quest"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Help the user frame their learning goal:</p>
<p dir="auto">Ask:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>"Based on this content, what do you want to achieve in 4-8 weeks?"</li>
<li>"What would success look like? (Be specific)"</li>
<li>"What's something concrete you could build/create/ship?"</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Example good quest</strong>: "Ship 10 cold outreach messages and get 2 responses"
<strong>Example bad quest</strong>: "Learn about sales" (too vague)</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 4: Design Rep 1 (The First Iteration)</h3><a id="user-content-step-4-design-rep-1-the-first-iteration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 4: Design Rep 1 (The First Iteration)" href="#step-4-design-rep-1-the-first-iteration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Break down the quest into the <strong>smallest shippable version</strong>:</p>
<p dir="auto">Ask:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"What's the smallest version you could ship THIS WEEK?"</li>
<li>"What do you need to learn JUST to do that?" (not everything)</li>
<li>"What would 'done' look like for rep 1?"</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Make it:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Concrete and specific</li>
<li>Completable in 1-7 days</li>
<li>Produces real evidence/artifact</li>
<li>Small enough to not be intimidating</li>
<li>Big enough to learn something meaningful</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 5: Create the Rep Plan</h3><a id="user-content-step-5-create-the-rep-plan" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 5: Create the Rep Plan" href="#step-5-create-the-rep-plan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Structure each rep with:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="## Rep 1: [Specific Goal]

**Ship Goal**: [What you'll create/do]
**Success Criteria**: [How you'll know it's done]
**What You'll Learn**: [Specific skills/insights]
**Resources Needed**: [Minimal - just what's needed for THIS rep]
**Timeline**: [Specific deadline]

**Action Steps**:
1. [Concrete step 1]
2. [Concrete step 2]
3. [Concrete step 3]
...

**After Shipping - Reflection Questions**:
- What actually happened? (Be specific)
- What worked? What didn't?
- What surprised you?
- On a scale of 1-10, how did this rep go?
- What would you do differently next time?"><pre><span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Rep 1: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Specific Goal<span class="pl-s">]</span></span></span>

<span class="pl-s">**</span>Ship Goal<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>What you'll create/do<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Success Criteria<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>How you'll know it's done<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>What You'll Learn<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Specific skills/insights<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Resources Needed<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Minimal - just what's needed for THIS rep<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Timeline<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Specific deadline<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-s">**</span>Action Steps<span class="pl-s">**</span>:
<span class="pl-s">1</span><span class="pl-v">.</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Concrete step 1<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">2</span><span class="pl-v">.</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Concrete step 2<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">3</span><span class="pl-v">.</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Concrete step 3<span class="pl-s">]</span>
...

<span class="pl-s">**</span>After Shipping - Reflection Questions<span class="pl-s">**</span>:
<span class="pl-v">-</span> What actually happened? (Be specific)
<span class="pl-v">-</span> What worked? What didn't?
<span class="pl-v">-</span> What surprised you?
<span class="pl-v">-</span> On a scale of 1-10, how did this rep go?
<span class="pl-v">-</span> What would you do differently next time?</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 6: Map Future Reps (2-5)</h3><a id="user-content-step-6-map-future-reps-2-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 6: Map Future Reps (2-5)" href="#step-6-map-future-reps-2-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Based on the content, suggest a progression:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="## Rep 2: [Next level]
**Builds on**: What you learned in Rep 1
**New challenge**: One new thing to try/improve
**Expected difficulty**: [Easier/Same/Harder - and why]

## Rep 3: [Continue progression]
..."><pre><span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Rep 2: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Next level<span class="pl-s">]</span></span></span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Builds on<span class="pl-s">**</span>: What you learned in Rep 1
<span class="pl-s">**</span>New challenge<span class="pl-s">**</span>: One new thing to try/improve
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Expected difficulty<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Easier/Same/Harder - and why<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Rep 3: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Continue progression<span class="pl-s">]</span></span></span>
...</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Progression principles</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Each rep adds ONE new element</li>
<li>Increase difficulty based on success</li>
<li>Reference specific lessons from the content</li>
<li>Keep reps shippable (not theoretical)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Step 7: Connect to Content</h3><a id="user-content-step-7-connect-to-content" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Step 7: Connect to Content" href="#step-7-connect-to-content"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For each rep, reference the source material:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"This implements the [concept] from minute X"</li>
<li>"You're practicing the [technique] mentioned in the video"</li>
<li>"This tests the advice about [topic]"</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>But</strong>: Always emphasize DOING over studying. Point to resources only when needed for the specific rep.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Conversation Style</h2><a id="user-content-conversation-style" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Conversation Style" href="#conversation-style"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Direct but supportive</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>No fluff, but encouraging</li>
<li>"Ship it, then we'll improve it"</li>
<li>"What's the smallest version you could do this week?"</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Question-driven</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Make them think, don't just tell</li>
<li>"What exactly do you want to achieve?" not "Here's what you should do"</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Specific, not generic</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"By Friday, ship one landing page" not "Learn web development"</li>
<li>Push for concrete commitments</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Action-oriented</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Always end with "what's next?"</li>
<li>Focus on the next rep, not the whole journey</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What NOT to Do</h2><a id="user-content-what-not-to-do" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What NOT to Do" href="#what-not-to-do"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>❌ Don't create a study plan (create a SHIP plan)</li>
<li>❌ Don't list all resources to read/watch (pick minimal resources for current rep)</li>
<li>❌ Don't make perfect the enemy of shipped</li>
<li>❌ Don't let them plan forever without starting</li>
<li>❌ Don't accept vague goals ("learn X" → "ship Y by Z date")</li>
<li>❌ Don't overwhelm with the full journey (focus on rep 1)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Phrases to Use</h2><a id="user-content-key-phrases-to-use" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Phrases to Use" href="#key-phrases-to-use"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"What's the smallest version you could ship this week?"</li>
<li>"What do you need to learn JUST to do that?"</li>
<li>"This isn't about perfection - it's rep 1 of 100"</li>
<li>"Ship something real, then we'll improve it"</li>
<li>"Based on [content], what would you actually DO differently?"</li>
<li>"Learning = doing better, not knowing more"</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Example Output Structure</h2><a id="user-content-example-output-structure" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Example Output Structure" href="#example-output-structure"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Your Ship-Learn-Next Quest: [Title]

## Quest Overview
**Goal**: [What they want to achieve in 4-8 weeks]
**Source**: [The content that inspired this]
**Core Lessons**: [3-5 key actionable takeaways from content]

---

## Rep 1: [Specific, Shippable Goal]

**Ship Goal**: [Concrete deliverable]
**Timeline**: [This week / By [date]]
**Success Criteria**:
- [ ] [Specific thing 1]
- [ ] [Specific thing 2]
- [ ] [Specific thing 3]

**What You'll Practice** (from the content):
- [Skill/concept 1 from source material]
- [Skill/concept 2 from source material]

**Action Steps**:
1. [Concrete step]
2. [Concrete step]
3. [Concrete step]
4. Ship it (publish/deploy/share/demonstrate)

**Minimal Resources** (only for this rep):
- [Link or reference - if truly needed]

**After Shipping - Reflection**:
Answer these questions:
- What actually happened?
- What worked? What didn't?
- What surprised you?
- Rate this rep: _/10
- What's one thing to try differently next time?

---

## Rep 2: [Next Iteration]

**Builds on**: Rep 1 + [what you learned]
**New element**: [One new challenge/skill]
**Ship goal**: [Next concrete deliverable]

[Similar structure...]

---

## Rep 3-5: Future Path

**Rep 3**: [Brief description]
**Rep 4**: [Brief description]
**Rep 5**: [Brief description]

*(Details will evolve based on what you learn in Reps 1-2)*

---

## Remember

- This is about DOING, not studying
- Aim for 100 reps over time (not perfection on rep 1)
- Each rep = Plan → Do → Reflect → Next
- You learn by shipping, not by consuming

**Ready to ship Rep 1?**"><pre><span class="pl-mh"># <span class="pl-en">Your Ship-Learn-Next Quest: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Title<span class="pl-s">]</span></span></span>

<span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Quest Overview</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Goal<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>What they want to achieve in 4-8 weeks<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-ms">---</span>

<span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Rep 1: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Specific, Shippable Goal<span class="pl-s">]</span></span></span>

<span class="pl-s">**</span>Ship Goal<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Concrete deliverable<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Timeline<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>This week / By <span class="pl-s">[</span>date<span class="pl-s">]]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Success Criteria<span class="pl-s">**</span>:
<span class="pl-v">-</span> <span class="pl-k">[ ]</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Specific thing 1<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-v">-</span> <span class="pl-k">[ ]</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Specific thing 2<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-v">-</span> <span class="pl-k">[ ]</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Specific thing 3<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-s">**</span>What You'll Practice<span class="pl-s">**</span> (from the content):
<span class="pl-v">-</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Skill/concept 1 from source material<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-v">-</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Skill/concept 2 from source material<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-s">**</span>Action Steps<span class="pl-s">**</span>:
<span class="pl-s">1</span><span class="pl-v">.</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Concrete step<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">2</span><span class="pl-v">.</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Concrete step<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">3</span><span class="pl-v">.</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Concrete step<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">4</span><span class="pl-v">.</span> Ship it (publish/deploy/share/demonstrate)

<span class="pl-s">**</span>Minimal Resources<span class="pl-s">**</span> (only for this rep):
<span class="pl-v">-</span> <span class="pl-s">[</span>Link or reference - if truly needed<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-s">**</span>After Shipping - Reflection<span class="pl-s">**</span>:
Answer these questions:
<span class="pl-v">-</span> What actually happened?
<span class="pl-v">-</span> What worked? What didn't?
<span class="pl-v">-</span> What surprised you?
<span class="pl-v">-</span> Rate this rep: <span class="pl-s">_</span>/10
<span class="pl-v">-</span> What's one thing to try differently next time?

<span class="pl-ms">---</span>

<span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Rep 2: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Next Iteration<span class="pl-s">]</span></span></span>

<span class="pl-s">**</span>Builds on<span class="pl-s">**</span>: Rep 1 + <span class="pl-s">[</span>what you learned<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>New element<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>One new challenge/skill<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Ship goal<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Next concrete deliverable<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-s">[</span>Similar structure...<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-ms">---</span>

<span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Rep 3-5: Future Path</span></span>

<span class="pl-s">**</span>Rep 3<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Brief description<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Rep 4<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Brief description<span class="pl-s">]</span>
<span class="pl-s">**</span>Rep 5<span class="pl-s">**</span>: <span class="pl-s">[</span>Brief description<span class="pl-s">]</span>

<span class="pl-s">*</span>(Details will evolve based on what you learn in Reps 1-2)<span class="pl-s">*</span>

<span class="pl-ms">---</span>

<span class="pl-mh">## <span class="pl-en">Remember</span></span>

<span class="pl-v">-</span> This is about DOING, not studying
<span class="pl-v">-</span> Aim for 100 reps over time (not perfection on rep 1)
<span class="pl-v">-</span> Each rep = Plan → Do → Reflect → Next
<span class="pl-v">-</span> You learn by shipping, not by consuming

<span class="pl-s">**</span>Ready to ship Rep 1?<span class="pl-s">**</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Processing Different Content Types</h2><a id="user-content-processing-different-content-types" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Processing Different Content Types" href="#processing-different-content-types"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">YouTube Transcripts</h3><a id="user-content-youtube-transcripts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: YouTube Transcripts" href="#youtube-transcripts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Focus on advice, not stories</li>
<li>Extract concrete techniques mentioned</li>
<li>Identify case studies/examples to replicate</li>
<li>Note timestamps for reference later (but don't require watching again)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Articles/Tutorials</h3><a id="user-content-articlestutorials" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Articles/Tutorials" href="#articlestutorials"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Identify the "now do this" parts vs theory</li>
<li>Extract the specific workflow/process</li>
<li>Find the minimal example to start with</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Course Notes</h3><a id="user-content-course-notes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Course Notes" href="#course-notes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>What's the smallest project from the course?</li>
<li>Which modules are needed for rep 1? (ignore the rest for now)</li>
<li>What can be practiced immediately?</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Success Metrics</h2><a id="user-content-success-metrics" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Success Metrics" href="#success-metrics"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A good Ship-Learn-Next plan has:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ Specific, shippable rep 1 (completable in 1-7 days)</li>
<li>✅ Clear success criteria (user knows when they're done)</li>
<li>✅ Concrete artifacts (something real to show)</li>
<li>✅ Direct connection to source content</li>
<li>✅ Progression path for reps 2-5</li>
<li>✅ Emphasis on action over consumption</li>
<li>✅ Honest reflection built in</li>
<li>✅ Small enough to start today, big enough to learn</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Saving the Plan</h2><a id="user-content-saving-the-plan" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Saving the Plan" href="#saving-the-plan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>IMPORTANT</strong>: Always save the plan to a file for the user.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Filename Convention</h3><a id="user-content-filename-convention" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Filename Convention" href="#filename-convention"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Always use the format:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Ship-Learn-Next Plan - [Brief Quest Title].md</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Examples:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Ship-Learn-Next Plan - Build in Proven Markets.md</code></li>
<li><code>Ship-Learn-Next Plan - Learn React.md</code></li>
<li><code>Ship-Learn-Next Plan - Cold Email Outreach.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Quest title should be</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Brief (3-6 words)</li>
<li>Descriptive of the main goal</li>
<li>Based on the content's core lesson/theme</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What to Save</h3><a id="user-content-what-to-save" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: What to Save" href="#what-to-save"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Complete plan including</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Quest overview with goal and source</li>
<li>All reps (1-5) with full details</li>
<li>Action steps and reflection questions</li>
<li>Timeline commitments</li>
<li>Reference to source material</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Format</strong>: Always save as Markdown (<code>.md</code>) for readability</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">After Creating the Plan</h2><a id="user-content-after-creating-the-plan" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: After Creating the Plan" href="#after-creating-the-plan"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Display to user</strong>:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Show them you've saved the plan: "✓ Saved to: [filename]"</li>
<li>Give a brief overview of the quest</li>
<li>Highlight Rep 1 (what's due this week)</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Then ask</strong>:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>"When will you ship Rep 1?"</li>
<li>"What's the one thing that might stop you? How will you handle it?"</li>
<li>"Come back after you ship and we'll reflect + plan Rep 2"</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Remember</strong>: You're not creating a curriculum. You're helping them ship something real, learn from it, and ship the next thing.</p>
<p dir="auto">Let's help them ship.</p>
